Resolutions of the Third Plenary Session

The Kuomintang's Third Plenary Session deliberated and resolved on various cases yesterday, the 3rd: (1) Work Guidelines for Training Party Members; (2) Promoting Party Affairs Work; (3) He Yingqin's proposal for a thrift movement; (4) Regarding construction guidelines. The original text of each case is recorded below:

Work Guidelines for Training Party Members

(I) Explanation

Party member training is the basic work of party departments at all levels. Since the Fourth Plenary Session of the Second Central Executive Committee, party departments at all levels have established special departments or sections to handle party member training. However, for the past two years, local party departments have generally emphasized superficial work in party member training, lacking practical effectiveness, resulting in repeated mistakes and frequent disputes. The errors are listed as follows: (1) Superficial understanding of doctrine, low level of knowledge, too little work experience, ignorance of obeying the public opinion of the majority and implementing party resolutions to achieve the party's overall action. Therefore, their unity is not solid; (2) Failure to understand the legacy of Dr. Sun Yat-sen’s universal love, using hatred as a psychology, destruction as a goal, even following the old tricks of the Communist Party, using the people as tools for struggle; (3) Too isolated from the history of the party; (4) Unwilling to pay attention to awakening people, nor willing to learn with an open mind; (5) Too small a vision, too narrow a mind, so often focusing on trivial matters, failing to grasp the big picture, or being clear about blaming others but ignoring self-criticism, even being fond of courage and fighting, engaging in personal disputes, and neglecting all party affairs development, social progress, or even abandoning them; (6) Too high a desire for leadership, so lazy in serving, brave in seizing, willing to sacrifice the interests of the entire nation for personal gain, and even thinking that the masses can be used by them, not knowing that they themselves are being used by others; (7) Not humbly observing the actual demands of the people, not sincerely doing practical work for the people, so unable to approach the people and gain their sympathy; (8) Often paying lip service to overthrowing bad gentry and local tyrants, but being used by bad gentry and local tyrants, and also failing to understand the reasons for the formation of bad gentry and local tyrants, so becoming bad gentry and local tyrants without realizing it; (9) Not energetic, doing things too slowly, unconsciously falling into corrupt habits; (10) Not distinguishing between public and private matters, with personal feelings of discord affecting the progress of party affairs, harming the public for personal gain, and avenging private grievances under the guise of public duty.

(II) Measures

The future direction of training party members should start with spiritual education, so that party members understand their position in society and their responsibilities, cultivate their sound personality, and firmly establish their belief in doctrine, fundamentally correcting their erroneous psychology and naive actions. The following points should be given practical attention by every party member when training party members: (1) Party members must know that improving party authority lies in their sound personality, academic cultivation, and sufficient ability. If they gain the trust of the people in society, then they can lead the people to practice doctrine. If they do not work hard in practical work, but only use the slogan of improving party authority to call on the masses, it will harm the development of party affairs; (2) Party members must strive to serve the society, so that local education, economic undertakings, can develop, then the people will naturally develop faith, and the special status of bad gentry and local tyrants in politics or economics will naturally not exist; (3) Party members must take service as their purpose, not seizure as their purpose; (4) Party members are the teachers of the people and should go to schools to educate young people and to society to educate the masses; (5) Party members must pay attention to approaching the people, publicizing doctrine, and influencing people's hearts, so that the people are sincerely convinced. Their attitude must be kind, so that they can gain the sympathy and trust of the people, and the progress of party affairs work will naturally reduce obstacles; (6) Party members should feel that their own abilities are insufficient, so they will be humble, and pay attention to developing creative abilities, so they can make progress.

Promoting Party Affairs Work

(I) Explanation

Since the Fourth Plenary Session of the Second Central Executive Committee decided to reorganize party affairs, the work of party departments at all levels has gradually moved from being scattered and disorganized to being orderly and unified. Some local party departments have been able to adhere to the central government's intentions and abide by the central government's laws and regulations to achieve results. However, the majority has not yet been able to get on the right track. The reasons for this are that they either lack work plans and concrete plans, or they do not understand the handling procedures and implementation methods, inverting priorities and confusing steps, resulting in increasingly empty party affairs work and declining party authority. The errors are listed below: (1) Emphasizing written work but lacking practical activities; (2) Emphasizing superficial propaganda but lacking practical achievements; (3) Emphasizing formal compliance but lacking work effectiveness; (4) Lacking correct training and guidance for party members; (5) Not recognizing the boundaries between the Executive Committee and the Supervisory Committee, so their work often has the drawback of duplication; (6) Not recognizing the boundaries between the party department and the government, resulting in disputes and conflicts between the party and the government; (7) Unable to lead the people, strive for social reform, and promote political progress; (8) Responsible personnel, due to their efforts in the work of their主管 (zhuguan - in charge of) department, have neglected to liaise and coordinate with other departments, resulting in畸形 (jixing - abnormal) development, and even the work of each department itself is hindered.

(II) Measures

In the future, methods for promoting party affairs work in various places must learn from past mistakes, remedy deficiencies, so that the organization is严密 (yanmi - tight/careful), the application is灵活 (linghuo - flexible), everyone uses their talents, and everything is done. Then the people will begin to believe, the party authority can be improved, and politics and society can be reformed. Based on this meaning, the main points are drafted as follows: (1) Executive committee members and supervisory committee members of party departments at all levels must not leave their posts without authorization, and service regulations should be promulgated for compliance; (2) All higher-level party departments should轮调 (luntiao - rotate and transfer) committee members of lower-level party departments to report on the status of party affairs work and provide necessary guidance and corrections, so as to receive the effect of contact and avoid the弊 (bi - drawbacks) of隔阂 (gehe - estrangement); (3) Party departments at all levels must focus on practical work and strive to serve the people in the future, so as to reform society and promote politics; (4) The circumstances in various places are not completely the same, and the types of work and their implementation procedures will naturally not be completely the same. Higher-level party departments should酌量 (zhuoliang - consider) the current situation in various places, separately formulate plans, instruct機宜 (jiyi - important matters),督促 (dūcù - supervise) implementation. Those formulated by the party departments themselves must be submitted to the higher-level party department for approval; (5) The types of work in lower-level party departments should be simple and easy to implement, and should not be too complicated. If too many matters are started at the same time, it will inevitably lead to顾此失彼 (gùcǐshībǐ - to attend to one thing and lose another), and no results will be achieved. Therefore, higher-level party departments should統盤 (tǒngpán - comprehensively) plan and formulate concrete plans, and gradually instruct lower-level party departments to implement them according to the prescribed procedures, so as to concentrate their efforts and計日觀成 (jìrìguānchéng - to look forward to completion every day); (6) Party affairs work must be in line with its time, place, and nature. Whether it is public or secret, it must be斟酌 (zhēnzhuó - considered) according to the situation, and should not adhere to a fixed view; (7) Party affairs work should be for construction purposes and should avoid attacking individuals. Special attention should be paid to comrades; (8) The supervisory committees of provincial and county party departments must pay attention to collecting evidence for举报 (jǔbào - report) cases. Therefore, they should first implement严密 (yanmi - tight/careful) supervision and must go through慎重 (shènzhòng - careful) review. Otherwise, empty言 (yan - words)举报 (jǔbào - report) will lead to谩骂 (mànmà - abuse), not only will it not补 (bǔ - help) the facts, but it will also损落 (sǔnluò - damage) the party's credibility; (9) Party departments at all levels should pay attention to increasing practical work and should not be limited to written work; (10) Party departments at all levels should send personnel to give lectures to each other to激励 (jīlì - encourage); (11) Party departments in counties and below must pay attention to developing the spirit of party members to serve the party. The daily party affairs work should be based on the principle of委员 (wěiyuán - committee members) and所属 (suǒshǔ - affiliated) party members using their职业 (zhíyè - professional) spare time to share the work. County party departments should reduce staff, and party departments below the county level must not employ staff unless there is an异常 (yichang - unusual) need and with the permission of the higher-level party department. If the living expenses of party affairs workers are reduced and the party's activities are increased, it will be easier to develop party affairs; (12) Party departments in counties and below must pay attention to developing the spirit of party members to serve the society, so that they engage in promoting public education and assisting local自治 (zìzhì - self-government) work, so as to gain the trust of the people and improve the dignity of the party.

Proposal for a Thrift Movement

At this time of national financial difficulties and economic hardship for the people, in order to increase political and economic effectiveness, enrich the national strength, and enrich the lives of the people, Yingqin believes that it is necessary to vigorously implement a thrift movement. In addition to separately explaining the reasons and significance of the thrift movement, based on this view, I respectfully propose the following to determine whether it is feasible: (A) For the government: (1) All central and provincial schools and institutions that are not urgently needed for訓政 (xùnzhèng - political tutelage) construction should be裁併 (cáibìng - reduced and merged); (2) Central and provincial institutions should strive to eliminate redundant personnel. Anyone employed must have a certain important position and cannot虚拟 (xūnǐ - fictitious) positions, position idle曹 (cao - officials), and remain韬 (tāo - hidden) the积习 (jixi - accumulated habits) of因人设事 (yīnrénshèshì - create a position for someone); (3) The expenses required by central and provincial institutions should be重定 (chóngdìng - redefined) budgeted, striving to reduce spending on徒 (tú - vain) consumption and移作 (yizuò - transferred to) construction expenses, or used to reward and subsidize various production undertakings; (4) Governments at all levels and various institutions, regardless of who is responsible, should pay attention to the effectiveness and results of their work in fact. All work that must be completed within a certain period within the scope of their responsibilities should be completed on schedule. If there are special故障 (gùzhàng - problems), the reasons should be申叙 (shēnshù - stated) in advance and核准 (hézhǔn - approved) by the central and higher-level agencies. Otherwise,因循 (yīnxún - delay) and贻误 (yíwù - mistakes) will be punished accordingly, and those responsible will have to自行引咎 (zìxíngyǐnjiù - offer to resign). (B) For the people: (1) Party departments at all levels should conduct extensive publicity for the thrift movement, so that the general public understands its benefits for individuals, society, and the country; (2) Prohibit various improper and wasteful entertainment, such as gambling, prostitution, smoking, and drinking; (3) All weddings, funerals, and celebrations should eliminate繁文缛节 (fánwénrùjié - unnecessary formalities) and advocate thrift. Within the possible range, agencies and various organizations should stipulate a considerable amount, so that the general public will not affect the stability of their lives due to应酬 (yìngchóu - social engagements); (4) Advocate or stipulate the use of domestic products, starting with personnel serving in the party, military, and government, and students in various schools, and then extending to various organizations, so that it is普及 (pǔjí - widespread) to the national people; (5) Find ways to promote postal savings, establish savings banks and industrial cooperatives, or other institutions of the same nature, so as to arouse interest in thrift and use the thrift expenses to increase production. (Explanation omitted)

Proposal on Construction Guidelines

The revolution focuses on destruction, but especially on construction after destruction. Dr. Sun Yat-sen's (International Joint Development of Chinese Industry Plan) has shown us the way to construction. Speaking of construction, there are countless matters, and it cannot be achieved overnight. In order to seek reality and not fall into empty talk, we can only choose the most urgent needs and gradually promote them. In terms of needs, laying railways, improving water conservancy, operating industries, developing mining, and扶植 (fúzhí - supporting) agriculture and commerce are all urgent plans at the moment, and cannot be delayed. However, among them, great construction undertakings such as railways, water conservancy, shipbuilding, iron making, and steel refining should be operated by the state in accordance with Dr. Sun Yat-sen’s meaning of节制资本 (jiézhìzīběn - limiting capital). If the national treasury is insufficient, it is necessary to borrow foreign capital within the scope of not hindering national sovereignty. Borrowing foreign capital for the purpose of兴利 (xìnglì - promoting benefits) is Dr. Sun Yat-sen’s advocacy, and we firmly believe that it can be implemented without弊 (bi - drawbacks). Looking around the country, the people's livelihood is declining, and哀鴻遍野 (āihóngbiànyě - cries of starving people) is everywhere. To solve倒悬 (dàoxuán - hanging upside down) to get out of水火 (shuǐhuǒ - deep trouble), there is no other way than construction. Taking Dr. Sun Yat-sen’s spirit of building the country with the party, and establishing a permanent foundation for the country, the recent construction guidelines are formulated as follows: (1) In accordance with Dr. Sun Yat-sen’s plan, pay attention to railway construction and water conservancy and electrical construction; (1) Dr. Sun Yat-sen’s industrial plan focuses on agriculture. All development of the Northeast and Northwest and整理 (zhěnglǐ - organize) waterways are for the sake of China’s agriculture. Therefore, the party should pay special attention to the development of agriculture in the future; (1) Chinese farmers account for more than 80% of the country’s population. Therefore, the government should pay special attention to farmer education in its education方針 (fāngzhēn - guiding policy), so that agricultural production is developed and agricultural affairs are振興 (zhènxīng - promote); (1) Strive to promote agricultural cooperation; (1) Each province should establish agricultural banks within a time limit to support the development of the rural economy; (1) Coal and iron mines that have been mined with results and have no逆产 (nìchǎn - contraband) relationship should be allowed to continue mining. Those with逆产 (nìchǎn - contraband) relationship should only receive their逆股 (nìgǔ - black market share) as公私合办 (gōngsīhébàn - joint public-private venture). However, it is stipulated that the mining land is owned by the state. Within a certain number of years, the government will not take rent. After that, rent will be paid every year until a certain year when it is completely nationalized; (1) Coal, iron, oil, and copper mines that have not been developed are all operated by the state. The government may准 (zhǔn - allow) foreigners to invest or jointly establish companies within a certain range according to Dr. Sun Yat-sen’s International Development Industry Plan; (1) The採 (cǎi - extraction) of other special mines should be handled according to the contract signed with private individuals as stipulated by Dr. Sun Yat-sen; (1) China’s ordinary industry, within the scope of the government’s promoting agriculture, increasing raw materials, reducing the price of raw materials, and the government’s implementing protective tariffs, is allowed to develop freely; (1) China’s special industries, the factories that should be newly established in Dr. Sun Yat-sen’s industrial plan, are all planned and handled by the government, and foreign capital and talent can be borrowed; (1) The government should prepare within two years (1) a large-scale iron-making and steel-refining factory, (1) a shipyard, (1) an electrical machinery manufacturing factory, and foreign capital can be borrowed to establish them. (1) Party members should strive to support and promote the development of industry and agriculture, and assist the government to prohibit all illegal acts that破坏 (pòhuài - destroy) industry and agriculture.

Liu Heding's Division Arrives in Quanzhou

The Fujian matter will be decided after Zhang Qun returns to Beijing. A Xiamen dispatch states that the entire 56th Division has been ordered to concentrate in Quanzhou. The entire 168th Brigade, commanded by Gui Zhenyuan, arrived in the city of Quanzhou in batches starting on the 17th. The entire 167th Brigade, commanded by Liu Shangzhi, arrived in Quanzhou on the 21st, passing through Tong'an by land from Zhangzhou, and on the 22nd, they set off to Hui'an, which borders Xinghua. Division Commander Liu Heding, at 11:00 a.m. on the 21st, led the entire staff of the division headquarters, the directly subordinate special service battalion, the mortar team, the communications team, and the engineering team, more than a thousand people, and arrived in Xiamen by small steamer. After Liu landed, he visited Lin Guogeng, the naval garrison commander of Zhangzhou and Xiamen, and talked for an hour, then went to Anhai, and arrived in Quanzhou at 7:00 p.m. The followers also arrived in Quanzhou on the 22nd. The 166th Brigade, commanded by Chen Wantai, led Jiang Yan's regiment, and entered Quanzhou from Zhangzhou and Xiamen on the 22nd. Also, Chen's brigade's Tang Bangzhen's regiment arrived in Xiamen on the 22nd by two sea轮 (lún - ship)伏龙 (Fulong - Crouching Dragon) and 醒狮 (Xingshi - Awakening Lion) from Shantou, and転 (zhuǎn - turn)ed to Quanzhou by small轮 (lún - ship) on the 23rd and 24th. So the entire 56th Division has concentrated in Quanzhou. Now Liu's brigade is concentrated in Hui'an, Gui's brigade is stationed in Nan'an, and Chen's brigade is stationed in Quanzhou. It is rumored that Liu's division will continue to enter the provincial capital, but when Liu Heding passed through Xiamen, his参议 (cānyì - counselor) Zheng Naicheng代 (dài - acting) Liu to meet with reporters, and denied this, saying that the division is only ordered to集 (jí - gather)泉 (Quanzhou), and everything is according to the central government's order, and there is no continuation yet. It is heard that Liu's division's集 (jí - gather)泉 (Quanzhou) is indeed a step of the central government to solve the Fujian situation, but the method still needs to wait for Zhang Qun to return to Beijing and复命 (fùmìng - report on duty) before deciding. Zhang Qun was刺 (cì - assassinated) in the省 (sheng - province), and伤 (shang - injured) the副官 (fùguān - adjutant) Li Zhongxing. According to a dispatch from a division, the murderer's real name is Li Chengzhu. After being arrested, there are (江秀淸) characters on his汗衫 (hànshān - undershirt). Jiang is Lin Shouchang's party. The Public Security Bureau is afraid of involving many people. After the inquiry, it was not published and转送 (zhuǎnsòng - transfer)押 (yā - detain) to the Provincial Defense Command. Also, a省 (sheng - province) dispatch was received yesterday, Zhang Qun and Lu Xingbang contacted the Fujian situation, and Lu Xingbang proposed (1) The provincial committee should be解 (jiě - relieve) in two batches, the first batch is Cheng Shikui, Xu Xianshi, Zheng Baoqing and Wu Shu, and the second batch is Lin Zhiyuan and Chen Naiyuan; (2) The above six people will be sent to省垣 (shěngyuán - provincial capital) by Lu's troops (February 26).

Landslide at Qingfeng West Ridge, Haizhou

A Xuzhou dispatch states that last year, the Elephant Trunk ditch mountain in Haizhou had a strange split. The Qingfeng Ridge of Yuntai Mountain, which is the second highest peak of Yuntai, with strange rocks and beautiful scenery, also collapsed a few days ago, with a thunderous sound that lasted for a long time. Nearby樵夫 (qiáofū - woodcutter), heard the sound胆落 (dǎnluò - terrified),奔逃 (bēntáo - fled) down the mountain. After climbing the mountain to察看 (chákàn - observe), they saw a section of Qingfeng West Ridge collapsed, about a hundred丈 (zhàng - a unit of length) long, and the trees under the mountain were all覆埋 (fùmái - buried).

青浦

Parents Break Engagement, Daughter Marries Herself: Chen Moushan, son of a villager surnamed Chen in Beigang Township, Qingpu, is 21 years old this year. At the age of nine, he was betrothed to the daughter of Wang Mou in Beiren Village. The woman is now 19. The engagement gifts were very meager at the time. Maoshan's family was poor, so he worked as a coolie in a factory in Shanghai to make a living. Now Wang, because she has a maternal cousin Ni Mou, whose family is not well-off, suddenly had the idea of disliking poverty and loving wealth. She insisted on breaking the engagement and promised her daughter to Ni Mou. The matter was heard by her daughter, who strongly disagreed. This woman was a staunch believer in the old ethics and felt very resentful in her heart. It happened that Maoshan returned to his hometown to visit relatives the other day, and she learned of it. She then met with her fiancé and vowed to marry Chen. However, Chen could not afford to marry her. Wang then eloped to the Chen family, willing to be a daughter-in-law and working very diligently, without complaining about the hardship. Wang only learned of the matter after losing his daughter and realized that there was nothing he could do.

Hall Order for Land Registration Within a Time Limit: The land registration matters in this county were handled by the County Finance Bureau in accordance with the order, starting from February 10th. Now the county government has received instructions from the Jiangsu Finance Department, requiring that it be reported within six months in accordance with the regulations. If the report is not submitted within the time limit, the verified deeds will be subject to a fee, and unverified deeds will be subject to double the penalty. If the report is not true, the excess land found during the land survey will be confiscated. As for the registration certificate, the numbers should be recorded according to the area.

Beaten Up, Good Dream Shattered: Lu Yadong of Chonggu Town, Qingpu, has been working in the Nanyishoutang Pharmacy in the town. He is already over forty years old and still unmarried, but he likes to wander around. He has a long-standing affair with Qiu, the wife of Zhou Mou. Qiu is in her twenties and quite beautiful. The residents of the town all know about it, but Zhou has no idea. The other day, Zhou went out on business, and Qiu invited Lu to a secret meeting again. Just as they were about to fulfill their dream, Zhou returned home unexpectedly and saw the scene. He was furious, grabbed Lu and beat him severely. Neighbors heard the noise and came to dissuade him, and only then was Lu released. Some say it was Lu's retribution for being lustful.

Changzhou

Four-District Robbery and Assault Case: At the home of Ding Shangen in Nanxiatian Village, Changchun Township, Fourth District of Wujin County, more than ten bandits arrived at about 10 p.m. one night. All were armed with handguns and flashlights. They forced Ding Shangen to hand over silver dollars. When he refused, they opened fire. Shangen was shot and fell to the ground. All his clothes and silver dollars were robbed. The bandits then went to the home of Ding's younger brother, Yangen, to rob. Yangen happened to be in Shanghai. His farmhand came out and shouted for help and was shot by the bandits and died immediately.

Huang District Chief Granted Bail: Zhu, the county magistrate of Wujin, previously received an order from the provincial government to keep Huang Gongwang, the chief of the Fifth District, under supervision in the county government club room. It has been more than a month. The county government has investigated and found that there was no plaintiff, and the accusations against him were also false. County Magistrate Zhu reported the situation to the provincial government, which then ordered that a reliable guarantor be obtained for his release. Huang District Chief was released on bail on March 2nd and resumed his original post.

Jingjiang

Kidnappers Throw Victims into the River: Yang Laowu, Zhu Jin, Yatou, and others were boatmen at Xi Si Wei Port in Zhengdongwei. At 3 p.m. on the 26th, as their boat was about to enter the port, a steamer suddenly approached, carrying seven or eight people with box cannons who opened fire along the way. When they reached the boat, the bandits jumped onto Yang's boat, robbed all the property, and kidnapped Yang Laowu, Zhu Jin, and Yatou. They cried for help, but the bandits were enraged and stripped them of their clothes and threw them into the Yangtze River. Their bodies have not been found yet.

Collection of Agricultural Improvement Surtax: The Finance Department issued an order that all counties where the land tax does not exceed 1% of the land price may collect an agricultural improvement surtax of 2%. This county has not exceeded the limit, and it was decided at the 42nd county government meeting that it will be implemented from 19th year.

Nantong

Fierce Battle Between Police and Bandits in Yu Xi: A bandit uprising occurred in Yu Xi District on the 1st, resulting in burning, looting, and killing, causing a terrible disaster. The telephone lines in the eastern township were all cut off by the bandits. The county police team rushed to suppress them and engaged in a fierce battle near Sijiaba. There were more than 300 bandits, who resisted fiercely. It was not until the afternoon of the 2nd that the bandits were driven back.

Another Dispute at Dada Small Wheel Company: A labor dispute occurred at the Dada Inland Small Wheel Company at the end of last year. The county government ruled that the company's board of directors should resolve it, but no results have been achieved. Shi Fengming, the executive committee member of the labor union, has accused Jiang Xiatang, the manager, of selling soil and smoking opium to the county government. It is not known how it will be resolved.

Jiangyin

Accumulated Grain Funds Almost Entirely Transferred: The county government, considering that the Yicang Management Committee has been established, ordered that all accumulated grain under the management of the fund-raising office should be transferred to the committee to implement grain storage in accordance with the law. The Finance Bureau was specifically ordered to instruct Director Xia to comply. Xia reported that the accumulated grain deposits, excluding those borrowed for the purchase of firearms for the Public Security Team, totaled 2,149.8 yuan in Baochang, 4,141.88 yuan in Yongcheng, 7,582.1 yuan in Chengfeng, 934.83 yuan in the general account, and 3,205.933 yuan in Changhua. Because Director Yin Qian faced difficulties in local expenses, all deposits except those in Changhua had been used to offset 3,900 yuan in Yongcheng, 8,300 yuan in Chengfeng, and 2,000 yuan in Baochang. Currently, only the deposits in Changhua can be fully transferred. The remaining funds need to be recovered by the county government.

Order to Investigate the Daily Conduct of Bao Hansheng and Others: The county government received an order from the Department of Civil Affairs to arrest Bao Hansheng, Wang Yanbin, Zhang Lianfang, and Gu Di of Changjing.

After questioning by the county, they were handed over to the Public Security Bureau for custody. They were also guaranteed by Chen Jingzhan, the district chief of the Seventh District. Zhang Jian was summoned for questioning the other day. It was claimed that Zhang Yi had no son and that his son's name was Tongxian, who was studying at Guanghua University in Shanghai and did not participate in external affairs. Moreover, there was no Zhang Yi in this village. After questioning, the county government ordered him to withdraw. Yesterday (the 1st), this case was secretly investigated by the headquarters because it involved important matters. The Public Security Bureau Chief Zhang Pinquan was specifically ordered to investigate when Wang Tongfu left the country, what the daily conduct of Bao Hansheng and the other three was like, and whether there were any reactionary activities. A clear report must be submitted for verification.

Finance Department Orders Investigation of Illegal Levies: The Changhai Tax Sub-bureau previously established a ranking team near Huangtiangang to Nanwai to address the issue of congested boats during the winter drought. Later, a conflict arose with the Ship Industry Labor Union over the collection of membership fees. The Labor Union filed a complaint with the Finance Department, which ordered the county to investigate. The other day, someone was privately collecting membership fees again and reported it to the county. County Magistrate Shen commissioned Judge Tong Cheng to investigate. Yesterday (the 2nd), they went to the County Party Headquarters. Xu Jiang was away on a trip to the province, so Xing Jiewen, the former executive committee member, took over. It was said that the Ship Labor Union's collection of membership fees was not on file. Tong went to the Beiwai Tax Office to investigate. The ranking team was registered with the Finance Department in the 12th year of the Republic of China, charging 30 cents for boats with more than 300 stones and 20 cents for boats with less than 300 stones.

Two cents were charged for each pig. Upon arriving at the Ship Industry Labor Union, a notice for the collection of membership fees was found on the wall. The other morning, dense gunfire was heard at Siduizai on the opposite bank. Yesterday, the police bureau investigated and learned that it was an Anqing cargo ship carrying more than ten loads of opium being thrown into the river. A bandit ship rushed to retrieve it and fired warning shots. The opium belonged to local merchants from Jiangyin and Jingjiang, and one-third was stolen. A telegram was immediately sent to Gu Mou in Zhenjiang to find a way to negotiate.

Yangzhou

Electricity Company Repeatedly Accused: The Yangzhou Zhenyang Electric Light Company was previously accused by 36 industries, including local leather and silk merchants, of illegally increasing prices. The lawsuit has been going on for nearly three years and has not been completely resolved. Recently, the company revised its business regulations, which sparked another wave of protests over unpaid fuel fees. The other day, Xie Jiren and Xu Jiechun filed another complaint with the Construction Committee and the Department of Construction, accusing the company of using purple copper wires for its power lines, disregarding departmental regulations, disregarding local safety, occupying public and private land, and filling official ditches, causing the entire city to become a swamp after heavy rains. They requested an investigation. It is now heard that the Department of Construction has copied the original complaint and ordered the original investigator, Jin Pu, to investigate the case thoroughly.

Hu

Village Committee Member Shot and Killed by Bandits: At about 7 p.m. on the 26th, several bandits wearing black robes suddenly broke into the home of Chen Danian, the village committee member of Miaoqian Village near Lincheng Bridge in Hu County. They shot Chen several times, hitting his vital points, and Chen died. The bandits fled upon seeing Chen dead. The Linshui police arrived after hearing the news, but the bandits were gone.

Water Police Recover Kidnapped Victims: At about 6 p.m. the other day, several bandits armed with wooden shell guns suddenly arrived at the home of former provincial assemblyman Zhu Dingcheng outside the West Gate of Changxing in Hu County. They kidnapped Zhu's brothers, Luoren and Da. Wang, the captain of the 11th water police team stationed in the county, immediately led one or two detachments to guard the main roads. The next afternoon, they encountered the bandits at Xiaowu Mountain. The two sides exchanged fire and fought fiercely for an hour before the bandits were defeated and fled in all directions. The police arrested Liu Chuntong, one of the bandits, and rescued the two kidnapped victims on the spot. Upon interrogation, the bandit confessed that the ringleader was Abbot Yuan, who was near the Coal Railway. Captain Wang immediately sent people to search the area based on the confession and arrested Abbot Yuan. He is now being held at the Changxing Public Security Bureau pending investigation.

Pinghu

Strange Method for Treating Meningitis: Since meningitis was discovered in the four townships of this county, the epidemic has been spreading rapidly in recent times. Recently, someone returned from Luxu Town and reported that the town also had the disease. Later, someone invented a simple first-aid method that has saved countless lives. The method involves placing a live rooster on the patient's chest. The rooster will remain still and not eat. After a few hours, the illness will suddenly disappear. Even in extremely critical cases, it can be saved. The method seems very simple. However, some people in Xincun Town have tried the method and have also cured several people. It is not known what the principle is.

County Executive Committee Determined: The members of the County Party Headquarters Executive and Supervisory Committee were selected by the Fifth County Representative Assembly and submitted to the province for approval. It is now known that Zhang Tingzhi, Chen Di, Yu Kaijun, Yang Zaoshi, and Shen Pengnian have been approved as members of the County Executive Committee.

Xincun Town Robbed by Bandits: This morning (the 2nd) at about 4 a.m., the county government received a telegram from Siliqiao stating that Xincun Town was robbed by bandits last night and has not stopped this morning. County Magistrate Fang immediately contacted the Provincial Security Team to suppress and defend the area after receiving the telegram. The losses are said to be about tens of thousands of yuan. A special curfew has been declared in Pingdi.

Education News

Important News

Hebei Earnestly Promotes Mass Education

Shen Yinmo, the Director of Education of Hebei Province, has plans and methods for promoting mass education in the counties of the province and earnestly implements them. This can serve as a reference for other provinces in promoting mass education. Director Shen of the province submitted a document to the Ministry of Education stating that the promotion of mass schools is a fundamental plan for implementing mass education and is of utmost importance during this period of political tutelage. Since the resumption of duties last year, the office has vigorously promoted mass schools. In August of last year, it formulated the Hebei Province Implementation Rules for Mass Schools in accordance with the Main Points of the Mass School Regulations issued by the Ministry, taking into account the local conditions of the province, and issued a notice for implementation. In September, it formulated the Hebei Province Method for Establishing Mass Schools in Counties in Stages, dividing all counties in the province into eight levels according to population, wealth, and other differences. During the six years of political tutelage, it stipulated that each level of county should establish at least a certain number of mass schools each year. By the end of the political tutelage period, every village should have a school and everyone should be studying. At the same time, it also formulated the Hebei Province County Education Bureau Chiefs' Special Project Assessment Method for Handling Mass Schools, which were all issued for implementation. Now, the aforementioned rules and methods are being submitted to the Ministry for review and approval, in addition to being submitted separately to the Hebei Provincial Government. The Hebei Province Method for Establishing Mass Schools in Counties in Stages generally divides all counties in the province into eight levels according to the household population, wealth, and education status of each county and sets out a phased implementation plan: (1) In the 18th year, counties of level A (Luan County) should establish at least 140 mass schools, counties of level B (Fengrun and Daming) should establish 100 schools each, counties of level C (Tianjin and four other counties) should establish 70 schools each, counties of level D (Tong County and 21 other counties) should establish 60 schools each, counties of level E (Wanping and 32 other counties) should establish 50 schools each, counties of level F (Daxing and 51 other counties) should establish 40 schools each, counties of level G (17 counties) should establish 30 schools each, and counties of level H (Xinzhen) should establish 15 schools. (2) In the 19th year, counties of level A should establish 60 schools each, level B 50, level C 40, level D 30, level E 20, level F 15, level G 10, and level H 4. (3) From the 20th year onward, each county should increase the number of schools year by year according to the aforementioned proportions until the 23rd year. It is estimated that counties of level A should establish at least 440 mass schools each, counties of level B 350, counties of level C 270, counties of level D 210, counties of level E 150, counties of level F 115, counties of level G 80, and counties of level H 35. (4) The number of mass schools to be established in stages is the minimum. All those who have met or exceeded the quota should continue to proceed. The ultimate goal is to ensure that every village has a school and everyone has the opportunity to receive education. (5) Each county education bureau must formulate detailed methods for establishing mass schools in accordance with these methods and based on the actual situation of each county and submit them to the office for approval.

Shanghai Special Municipal Mass Schools, a total of 34 schools this semester.

The Luxing District Education Association held its first standing committee meeting at Xiangdao Elementary School yesterday. Chairman Wang Zhongcan presided over the meeting. If the substitute for the supervisory committee member is insufficient, it will be filled by a public vote at the general assembly. Municipal Rural Normal School Will Build New School Buildings

The Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau opened a Rural Normal School last year. Due to the haste, it was unable to build school buildings and temporarily used a portion of the buildings of the former Xinlu Municipal Jiazi Elementary School, which was inconvenient. The funds for the construction of the Rural Normal School's school buildings have been approved by the municipal government. The other day, the bureau sent Zhu Chun, together with personnel from the Public Works Bureau, to inspect the site and will soon invite bids for construction.

Municipal Schools Must Register with the Social Affairs Bureau for Afforestation Seedlings

The Municipal Education Bureau recently issued an order to all municipal schools, gymnasiums, school gardens, and mass education centers that, as the Afforestation Propaganda Week is approaching, municipal schools must obtain at least ten seedlings from the Social Affairs Bureau. However, each municipal school must first register with the Social Affairs Bureau the number of seedlings required and the type of seedlings that are suitable in order to facilitate verification and issuance.

The Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau's Business Report at the Sixth Municipal Congress (2)

(71) Continue intelligence testing and educational testing. Individual and group intelligence tests have been completed and two reports have been printed. Educational testing is in full swing.

(12) Implement college entrance guidance and employment guidance. Various survey forms were printed and sent to municipal schools and private schools that have been approved for registration, ordering graduates to fill them out and submit them for statistics. A guidance committee was also organized, with the appointment of section chiefs Yang Jiachun and Jiang Hongqi and the invitation of Mr. Chen Bulei and Mr. Wang Yunwu as members to handle the guidance of students for college entrance and employment.

(13) Repair school buildings in stages. Many municipal school buildings have been in disrepair for years or are insufficient. Due to the city's financial constraints, each school will collect construction fees, which will be kept in a special account by the Finance Bureau and used exclusively for repairing municipal school buildings. A school building repair committee will be organized by the bureau in conjunction with the Finance and Public Works Bureaus to plan the repair work. The municipal school buildings that have been completed are Chongzheng, Chaozong, and Bide. The ones under construction are Wanzhu, Fahua District 7, District 16, and Honglu. The ones being planned are the Rural Normal School, Cangji, and Yangzheng.

(14) Hold the Second Joint Elementary School Sports Meet. The city's first joint elementary school sports meet was held in the 17th year. On the birthday of Premier in the 18th year, the second joint elementary school sports meet was held, lasting for three days. Sixty-six municipal schools and nine private schools participated, with 8,445 students participating. About 10,000 to several thousand visitors came to watch each day. Many prizes were donated by groups and individuals. The results were also better than the previous event.

(15) Organize a Curriculum Research Committee for Elementary and Secondary Schools. The curriculum for elementary and secondary schools must be adapted to local needs and environmental conditions. Therefore, staff members of the bureau and educational experts were appointed to organize a Curriculum Research Committee for Elementary and Secondary Schools to carefully study and comply with the standards issued by the Ministry. The two committees held many meetings and have agreed on the subjects, types, and time allocation for elementary schools in the city, ordering each elementary school to comply with and conduct trials for one semester. After the end of the semester, the results of the trials will be submitted for review and approval. The curriculum standards for secondary schools are being studied by subject and will be agreed upon soon.

(16) Reorganize the Joint Association of Teachers and Staff in Each School. The organization of the Joint Association of Teachers and Staff in each municipal and private school in the city has been inconsistent. Unless it is reorganized, it will be difficult to unify it. The bureau has formulated Provisional Regulations for the Joint Association of Teachers and Staff in Municipal Schools in Each District, Preparatory Regulations, Provisional Regulations for the Joint Association of Teachers and Staff in Private Elementary and Secondary Schools, and Preparatory Regulations. First, each teachers' association will be ordered to suspend activities, and the municipal party headquarters will jointly select preparatory committee members for the municipal school teachers' associations in each district to prepare for the reorganization. Now, most of them have been formally established.

(17) Handle school health matters. (1) Formulate eight articles of a student hygiene habit plan for municipal elementary schools. The Health Bureau will compile two types of simple explanations of hygiene habits, and the bureau will formulate eight articles of measures to effectively implement them. (2) In conjunction with the Health Bureau, organize school health promotion associations in municipal schools, allocate funds, and actively proceed. (3) Carry out smallpox vaccination for students in municipal schools to prevent smallpox. (4) When meningitis occurred last year and epidemic diseases were discovered in the summer, each school was ordered to hold preventive injections to avoid infection.

(B) Regarding social education

(1) Literacy Movement. Organize a Literacy Movement Committee, plan implementation methods, give speeches on the need for literacy at any time, distribute literacy movement leaflets, and install oil-painted color-through educational picture signs and enamel popular education slogan signs in the City Temple and at key intersections to promote the self-awareness of unemployed people.

(2) Organize a Mass Education Committee. Most Chinese people lose their education in childhood. Mass education is indeed an essential plan for popularizing education. The guiding principles of the policy direction curriculum outline should be determined to serve as a standard. Therefore, a Mass Education Committee was organized to plan the overall responsibility of mass education.

National Games (1) Number of Participants in Nanjing

Approximately 120 athletes

All participate except for swimming

The Preparatory Office of the National Games received a letter from the Nanjing Special Municipal Education Bureau yesterday responding to the number of participants in the games. All items will be participated in except for swimming. The original letter is recorded as follows: Respectfully, I recently received your association's telegram regarding the opening of the meeting. The Nanjing Special Municipality Preparatory Committee for the National Games has been formally established, and all preparatory matters are actively underway. The Nanjing Special Municipality will send approximately 120 athletes to participate in the games. According to the trophies of the sports events set by your association, all events except swimming are planned to be prepared for participation. Once the preliminary selection is completed, the registration will be submitted on time. This is a reply in advance, hoping for your review.

(2) Accommodation and Food Prepared Properly

The conference anticipates that there will be thousands of athletes participating from various regions and that the number of conference staff will also be considerable. Therefore, the conference should properly address the issue of food and beverages in advance. The logistics department has invited merchants to contract the catering and has reportedly reached an agreement. However, for the sake of caution, the department has established a contract for the cleanliness of the meals, the size of the plates and bowls, and the amount of food to prevent malpractice from occurring in the future. Regarding the issue of accommodation, the department is also making proper preparations and has ordered the three major barracks originally located behind the Dayingpan to be repaired. It is expected that they will be completed within a few days. The interior finishing and all arrangements have been handled to ensure cleanliness and hygiene as the main priority.

(3) Business Market Begins Construction

The conference is also building houses in the venue to facilitate merchants to rent and operate stores. The conference anticipates that during the conference period, the average daily attendance of participants and visitors will be tens of thousands. The development of its business can be guaranteed. However, the purpose of the conference for the shops participating in the venue is to facilitate visitors. Therefore, extremely low rental fees are charged to receive great benefits. Therefore, major companies and stores in Shanghai have been rushing to reserve rentals. However, it is heard that some merchants plan to build their own buildings. Due to the imminent start of the conference, the conference has decided to order construction to be completed within the time limit to ensure uniformity.

(4) Soliciting Advertisements for the Handbook

In order to enable participating groups and people from all provinces to understand the content and the significance of the creation of the conference, the conference will issue a handbook for the National Games, which has been compiled and will be printed soon. In order to facilitate the business of major companies and merchants in each province, dozens of advertisement spaces have been specially reserved in the handbook at low prices for all walks of life to subscribe to.

Local News

Zhang Qun Returned to Shanghai Yesterday

Proper Arrangements Have Been Made for the Fujian Affairs.

The Provincial Committee Members Who Went to Beijing Were Punished.

Shanghai Special Municipality Mayor Zhang Qun returned to Shanghai from Fujian aboard the Puan warship on the evening of the 28th of last month. Due to fog, he only arrived at Wusongkou at 12:00 PM yesterday. Accompanying him were several staff members, including Lin Yannan. Secretary Guo Shihui, who went with him, is said to be returning to Shanghai in a week due to other business. Many people from the military and political circles of Shanghai welcomed him at the dock, including government officials and adjutants from the Naval Reorganization Office. After disembarking, Zhang went straight home by car to rest. At 3:30 PM, he went to the Municipal Government to work. A reporter from this newspaper interviewed him, and Zhang spoke in detail about the Fujian affairs. The details are as follows:

Investigation Results Zhang said, "I was ordered to go to Fujian to investigate and deal with the Provincial Committee dispute, and I was determined to uphold the authority of the Central Government and resolve local disputes. After arriving in Fujian with Chairman Yang, I sent staff to Youxi to inquire about everything from Lu Xingbang and conducted detailed investigations in all aspects. Only then did I realize the crux of the problem was entirely due to suspicion and misunderstanding. The rumors that one party was resisting the Central Government were not true. Therefore, I stayed in Fujian and consulted with Chairman Yang and others, and finally, we decided on a very proper way to resolve local disputes while maintaining the authority of the Central Government. Therefore, when I left Fujian, I telegraphed the results of the investigation and the methods of handling the aftermath to the Central Government for review and implementation."

Provincial Committee to be Sent to Beijing The telegram to the Central Government stated that after investigation, according to Lin Zhong, Sa Fuchou, etc., Lin Zhiyuan and five others were suspected of being reactionary, so they were arrested. However, Lin Zhong, Sa Fuchou, Lu Xingrong, and others acted arbitrarily in the arrest, violating regulations, and should be punished. As for the arrested Provincial Committee members Lin Zhiyuan, Xu Xianshi, Chen Naiyuan, Cheng Shiyue, Zheng Baoqing, and the Director of the Maritime Public Security Bureau, Wu Shu, and five others, they should be sent to the province and then to Nanjing, where the Central Government will conduct a thorough investigation to determine whether they have reactionary tendencies and then decide on their punishment.

Request for Punishment Zhang also said that this was his and others' opinion. It is still unknown whether the Central Government will agree or not. Lin Zhong, commander of the Provincial Defense Army, Sa Fuchou, commander of the fortress, and Lu Xingrong, provincial committee member, knew that arbitrary arrests were wrong and requested punishment. Today (March 3rd), I received a telegram from Fujian stating that Lin Zhiyuan and other provincial committee members would be sent to the province and then to Beijing soon, so the established plan must be carried out smoothly without any problems. I received a telegram from Lin Zhong and others on the boat, stating that rumors were rife outside, but they were sincerely supporting the Central Government and had no other intentions, asking me to explain to the Central Government on their behalf. Therefore, rumors that Lu Xingbang was spying on Zhejiang were not credible. Chairman Yang will probably not come to Beijing for the time being. The reorganization of the Fujian Provincial Government is a matter of fact.

Assassination Incident I was ordered to go to Fujian to investigate, but I had no rights to speak of, and I had no grudges against any individual in Fujian. Unfortunately, an assassination occurred after I arrived in Fujian, so it can be determined that it was a political act. Adjutant Li Zhonghang died as a result. Li had been with me for nearly five years and was very capable. It is a pity that he was killed suddenly. Li was shot in the car, but he was still able to jump out of the car and shoot at the assassins, falling to the ground after taking ten steps. The wounded assassin was shot in the left brain and was unconscious and unable to speak clearly, so there was no confession. Rumors that so-and-so was the mastermind are all speculations, not confirmed by the assassin himself. Li's coffin will be transported back to his ancestral home in Anhui by his father in a few days. Secretary Guo Shihui, who stayed in Fujian to liaise, will also return to Shanghai soon. Because the Third Plenary Session has no new proposals, I will go to Beijing after the municipal government affairs are cleared up.

Guo Shen's Telegram The municipal government received a telegram from Secretary Guo Shihui, who accompanied Mayor Zhang to Fujian, stating that after arriving in Fujian, he was assigned to Youxi to investigate the situation in all aspects. After the matter was completed, he returned to the province. The mayor maintained the authority of the Central Government and resolved local disputes, and drafted a plan to be submitted to the Central Government for approval. The arrested provincial committee members will be sent to the province within a few days. The mayor has already left for Shanghai. Shen will stay here for another week. (Signed) Guo Shen.

Ministry of Health Convened Sino-Foreign Epidemic Prevention Conference in Shanghai Yesterday

Many Important Cases Resolved

Emphasis on Customs Quarantine

Yesterday afternoon at 3:30, the Ministry of Health convened a joint Sino-foreign epidemic prevention conference at the Municipal Club on Weihaiwei Road, with the participation of health authorities from the concessions and directors and heads of various departments of the Ministry. Minister Liu Ruiheng personally came to Shanghai to attend. Many important epidemic prevention cases were resolved, and the meeting adjourned at around 6:00 PM. The details of the meeting are summarized below:

Attendees The Chinese attendees, in addition to Chairman Liu Ruiheng, included Health Director Cai Hong, Health Care Director Jin Baoshan, Director of the Central Hygiene Laboratory Chen Fangzhi, Director of the Shanghai Hygiene Laboratory Chen Jun, Director of the Hygiene Department of the Ministry of Railways Hu Xuanmin, Director of the Shanghai Special Municipality Hygiene Bureau Hu Hongji, and President of the Red Cross Hospital Yan Fuqing. The foreign attendees included Dr. Davis, Director of the Shanghai Municipal Council Health Bureau, Deputy Director Brijdon, Director-General of the French Concession Council Fotian Ya, and Director of the Customs Quarantine Office Ai Wuhua, and ten others.

Joint Epidemic Prevention Office The discussion then turned to epidemic prevention measures. It was agreed that as the weather was gradually warming up, cholera would soon be rampant. The prevention of cholera should be discussed first. It was decided that (1) a temporary joint cholera prevention office would be established by the Chinese and foreigners. The Ministry of Health would send personnel to preside over it, and the concession authorities would send representatives to participate. The first priority would be to investigate the origin of cholera and study isolation methods. Then, a unified form would be drafted. If a cholera patient was found, the doctor would report to the office using the form, and personnel would be dispatched immediately to investigate.

Designated Propaganda Day (2) Regarding hygiene education for cholera, emphasis should be placed on joint Sino-foreign propaganda. The poor residents on both sides of the Suzhou River in Shanghai are the source of cholera, so propaganda should start from these areas. May 15 was designated as propaganda day, and large-scale lectures and various propaganda activities would be held simultaneously in various locations.

Wusongkou Inspection (3) The Chinese and foreign authorities should strictly prohibit food and unclean river water, and pay special attention to preventive vaccinations for the poor. (4) An inspection station should be set up at Wusongkou to inspect various imported small boats. The Ministry of Health will allocate a certain amount of special funds each month to cover expenses.

Customs Quarantine Office The discussion continued until around 6:00 PM before adjourning. Minister Liu Ruiheng and Director Jin Baoshan took the train back to Beijing last night. According to a conversation with Jin Baoshan, the fundamental method of epidemic prevention is to focus on port quarantine. The Ministry of Health has decided to take over the Shanghai Customs Quarantine Office this summer.

After two years, the Ministry of Health will gradually take over various important ports. The Ministry is currently sending personnel to various European and American countries to conduct surveys and studies for reference. In addition, Director Yan Zhizhong of the Medical Administration Department has been sent to attend the International Health Conference held in Geneva on March 5.

Gold Prices Plunged Suddenly Yesterday

A Drop of Nearly Thirty Taels Compared to Last Saturday

The Great Evening News reported that this morning (March 3), the highest gold price at the opening of the market still reached 514 taels. However, in less than two hours, it fell to 488 taels and five qian, a drop of nearly 30 taels compared to last Saturday. Such a dramatic change is unprecedented since Shanghai had a gold market. The exchange rate also fluctuated as a result. Even banks were at a loss. It is said that today's sharp drop in gold prices was caused by the news of a proposal by several key figures in the banking industry to levy a tax on the import of silver. However, the Ministry of Finance has not yet decided whether to adopt this proposal, because the impact of the tax on the financial market has not been thoroughly studied. It is also said that some people argue that silver is currency in China, but goods in India, so their nature is different. The taxation issue should be given special consideration. It is difficult to say whether the benefits obtained after taxation will meet today's expectations. As a result of today's drastic changes in the gold market, Japanese banks sold off in large quantities after the market opened when rumors spread, and then bought in large quantities again at the close. General import and export merchants who wanted to settle prices were mostly at a loss and did not know what to do because the market situation was unpredictable.

Chamber of Commerce to Hold a Meeting to Maintain Industry

Meeting Decided for Afternoon of the 6th

Letters Sent to Various Industries Yesterday Asking Them to Send Representatives

Regarding the convening of a meeting to maintain industry, the Chamber of Commerce sent letters yesterday to relevant industry groups and all executive committee members, stating that the Chamber had previously noted that domestic industries had been stagnated last year due to various influences. The current situation is precarious. The shipping, silk mills, match factories, silk weaving, cotton weaving, cigarette factories, etc. cannot sustain themselves. Industry is the lifeblood of the country, and Shanghai is the national hub. National economy and the people's livelihood are very important. If we do not seek to save it urgently, the danger that is coming is unbearable to imagine. Executive Committee Member Qiaqing of this Chamber met with President Jiang of the National Government in Beijing on February 4 to explain the pros and cons in detail and ask the government to provide relief. The President appreciated it very much.

He instructed us to return to Shanghai, put forward a plan, and submit it for adoption. The 37th Executive Committee Meeting of this Chamber resolved to submit the matter to the 10th Plenary Committee Meeting for discussion. It was agreed that it is the Chamber's duty to maintain industry, and we should actively plan. However, the situation of each industry is different, and the methods should also be different. The principles of this case were unanimously passed. As for the detailed methods, the Standing Committee was instructed to convene representatives of each industry to discuss and decide on them before making suggestions to the government. Therefore, the meeting will be held at 1:30 PM on Thursday, March 6, in the Chamber's Standing Committee Room to convene representatives of various industries. The chamber hopes that your organization will send one to three representatives to attend the meeting and discuss together. The future of industry and the lifeblood of the country are at stake. The Chamber hopes you will be present on time.

Compilation of Commemorative Weekly Meetings in Various Organizations

Municipal Party Headquarters: The Shanghai Special Municipal Party Headquarters held an expanded memorial week for the late Premier yesterday morning at 9:00 AM. Over 300 people attended, including representatives from the city-wide representative conference, representatives from various organizations, and staff members of the Municipal Party Headquarters. Pan Gongzhan presided, Xu Yefu served as the master of ceremonies, and Huang Xianggu and Bao Rong recorded the proceedings. After the customary rituals, Chen Dehui gave a political report, stating: "Comrades, last week, the Municipal Party Headquarters received an order from the Central Government, instructing us to hold an expanded memorial week to report on the Central Government's recent attitude and Yan Xishan's mistakes. The timing is excellent, as the city-wide representative conference just opened the day before yesterday, providing us with a perfect opportunity to hold this event. Now, let us discuss Yan Xishan's mistakes. Since Yan Xishan issued his telegram, there have been numerous and thorough condemnations from various quarters. We understand that Yan Xishan's apparent mistakes lie in the words of his telegram, such as 'Suppression of internal strife,' 'Courtesy and concession for the sake of the nation,' and 'Responsibility while out of office.' He declared his intention to resign while urging Comrade Chiang Kai-shek to resign as well. There has been much criticism regarding the point of 'courtesy and concession,' as he clearly misunderstands its meaning. We can analyze this from three aspects: (1) Only personal rights and interests can be subject to courtesy and concession, expressing humility and candor. However, the responsibility of pursuing the welfare of the masses cannot be subject to courtesy and concession. In other words, revolutionary causes and revolutionary responsibilities cannot be subject to courtesy and concession. How can the people's cause and responsibility be subject to courtesy and concession? Consider Zhuge Kongming, who, to maintain the legitimacy of the Han Dynasty, knew that Liu Adou was incapable, yet he dedicated himself to the cause, exhausting his efforts until his death, out of a sense of responsibility. Furthermore, the spirit of courtesy and concession was prevalent during the Three Dynasties, but mostly in times of peace. Based on past history and current circumstances, it is absolutely impermissible for anyone in a position of responsibility to talk about courtesy and concession. When the late Premier assumed the position of Provisional President, he relinquished power to Yuan Shikai to achieve national unity and peace. However, Yuan Shikai later plotted to usurp power, leading to internal warfare, resulting in fourteen years of chaos. The late Premier was deeply troubled by this. Now, if we were to allow anyone to talk about courtesy and concession with the foundation of the Party and the nation built upon the blood and sacrifice of all comrades and revolutionary masses, what would become of it? Those bearing the heavy responsibility of the Party and the nation absolutely cannot engage in courtesy and concession. Yan Xishan does not understand revolution and therefore makes such absurd statements. (2) His intention is actually to induce others to practice courtesy and concession, as he is surrounded by numerous strange and worthless politicians who incite him. He believes that if Comrade Chiang Kai-shek resigns, he will be embraced by others, leading to his absurd thinking. (3) His statement that he can take responsibility while out of office is factually untenable and extremely contradictory. How can one take responsibility while out of office? If one can take responsibility while out of office, then one can incite internal warfare. What responsibility do those in office bear? Yan Xishan truly lacks political common sense and revolutionary sentiment, leading to such absurd statements. If he genuinely wishes to talk about courtesy and concession, he can do so himself and resign. If he wishes to travel abroad, Feng Yuxiang is still waiting for him. Since he issued his telegram, not only has he not practiced the courtesy and concession he spoke of,

Page 14

he continues to dream of being an emperor in Shanxi, advocating for the establishment of a Privy Council and a Council of Elders, as well as the convening of meetings of all Central Committee sessions and a general vote of Party members. His statements are naturally motivated. If he wishes to go abroad, I believe the entire nation will welcome him. Let us now discuss his absurd proposals. He advocates for convening joint meetings of all Central Committee sessions and ordering a general vote of Party members, claiming that "Party matters should be left to Party members." If he considers the Third Plenary Session to be illegitimate, why does he want to convene the Third Central Committee session? Clearly, he knows that he was not a Central Committee member in the first two sessions, and if a meeting were held, he would have no place. The Municipal Executive Committee has already issued a condemning telegram. We understand that Party members do not have individual freedom but only Party freedom. His words and actions are truly acts of betrayal against the Party, aimed at overturning the Kuomintang. We should, of course, use Party discipline to severely punish him. He claims that in the first two Central Committees, many loyal comrades were expelled without cause. By this logic, the late Premier was wrong to deal with Chen Jiongming and to expel Yang Ximin and Liu Zhenhuan.

Why does he have such slanderous remarks against the Party? He is an opportunist. Since the beginning of the Republic, he has been an emperor in Shanxi. He could pay homage during the Hongxian era, and his position remained unshaken as various warlords rose to power. He wants to preserve his territory and, at this juncture, intends to engage in cunning rebellion in secret. We are well aware of his behind-the-scenes manipulations. This time, he attempts to repeat his old tricks and become audacious. He not only fails to recognize the Party but also greatly underestimates it. He believes our Party is an ordinary party, and revolutionary leaders are akin to warlords. He fails to understand that our Party has principles, and revolutionary leaders are unwavering, adhering to the teachings of the late Premier, dedicating their lives and abilities to the Party. We also understand that he is currently surrounded by all counter-revolutionary elements, causing such mistakes, and attempting to divide and disrupt the Party. In summary, he is accustomed to being an emperor and simply does not understand matters outside his domain, remaining an ignorant rustic. Now is the time for the struggle between revolution and counter-revolutionary feudal forces, and the quicker we eliminate them, the sooner the welfare of the Party and the people will be realized. As for the Central Government's attitude towards Yan Xishan, it is very stern. Knowing that he has not received adequate education, cultivation, and refinement, and fundamentally misunderstands the meaning of revolution, they intend to deal with him using the same method the late Premier used to deal with Chen Jiongming, repeatedly advising him and unwilling to let him sever ties with the Party. If it comes to the point of no return, naturally, Party discipline will be applied. The Third Plenary Session has already resolved to send personnel to investigate, demonstrating that the Central Government still wishes to help him and treat him with leniency. If he does not awaken, there will be stern measures to eliminate this traitor for the people. The end."

Holding of Afforestation Movement Week

The Jiangsu Provincial Education Department Orders County Governments to Instruct All Schools to Comply

The Shanghai County Government received an order from the Jiangsu Provincial Education Department yesterday, stating: "Regarding the matter of issuing an order, the Ministry of Education's Order No. 122 is now received, which states: 'According to the Executive Yuan's report, based on the proposal of Minister of Agriculture and Mining Yi Peiji, it is found that the Central Executive Committee promulgated the Measures for Grassroots Work Movement last year, listing afforestation movement as one of the seven movements. The Provisional Regulations on Tree Planting in Provinces, announced by the Ministry for the Commemoration of the Late Premier's Death by Tree Planting, also stipulate that each province should hold a tree planting ceremony and afforestation movement on March 12th each year, the anniversary of the Late Premier's death. However, the results at the beginning of implementation are not many. If it is not earnestly promoted, it is feared that it will become a mere formality over time. The anniversary of the Late Premier's death this year is approaching, and preparations for this afforestation movement should be made urgently. To expand the movement, it is proposed to designate one week, starting from March 11th, as the Afforestation Promotion Week, and to hold large-scale afforestation movements in the capital and the provincial and county governments, so as to popularize afforestation knowledge to the people of the whole country in the shortest possible time. The implementation methods are as follows: In the capital, it is proposed that the Ministry convene representatives from the Ministry of Interior, Ministry of Education, Ministry of Railways, Construction Commission, and the Nanjing Special Municipal Party Headquarters, Municipal Government, Central University College of Agriculture, Jinling University Department of Agriculture and Forestry, etc., to form a temporary committee for the afforestation movement in the capital, and to deliberate on the implementation. In the provinces, counties, and cities, the provincial, county, and city governments shall be responsible for handling the matter together with the provincial, county, and city Party headquarters. The Executive Yuan is requested to report to the National Government for approval, and to issue an order to all ministries and departments, and all provincial, municipal, and county governments to respectfully comply with, so as to commemorate and value forestry policy.' This was discussed and approved at the 50th meeting of this Yuan and decided to be implemented. In addition to sending a letter to the Secretariat of the Central Executive Committee for forwarding, we hereby report to your government for review and approval, and to issue an order to comply with the above. We also request that you instruct us to comply." According to this, it was immediately proposed to the 61st State Council meeting of this government, and it was resolved to follow the order, and to instruct the Executive Yuan to instruct the Ministry of Agriculture and Mining to forward the information to the provincial governments and special municipal governments, and to formulate and report the afforestation plans and completion dates of the provinces and cities. In addition to issuing instructions and distributing them, this order requires the Department to respectfully comply with it. This order, etc., is hereby issued. In addition to the distribution of orders, this order is hereby issued to the County Magistrate to respectfully comply with it and instruct all schools to comply with it. This order."

Tragic Disaster Situation in Xingping County, Shaanxi

Deaths Reach 71,691

Mr. Sun Weidong, representative of the Shanghai Shaanxi Relief Association, recently received a telegram from the Shaanxi Disaster Relief News Agency, reporting on the tragic disaster situation in Xingping County, Shaanxi Province. The original text is as follows: Shanghai No. 6 Malu office, transferred to Committee Member Sun Longji, Nanjing Fuxieshe, Guowenshe, Peiping Ma Zhixiang. After six heavy snowfalls in Shaanxi Province, the disaster situation in each county is increasingly severe. In Xingping County, the snow is more than three feet deep. In the northern villages of the county, such as Li Village, Ce Village, Yang Village, Zhoubian Village, West Wang Village, Zhangjia Village, and over thirty other villages, each village originally had a population of one hundred or two hundred, but today each village is empty, and all houses have been demolished, leaving not a single beam or piece of wood. The southern villages of the county are at lower elevations, and there was a harvest of one or two tenths last year due to artificial irrigation. However, more than eighty out of every hundred households are currently without food. Those who can maintain a livelihood for half a month account for 15-16 percent, and only one or two out of every hundred households can maintain until the spring wheat harvest. Out of the original population of 176,685 in the entire county, the number of deaths has reached 71,691, and 3,288 households have been wiped out. Although the Relief Association has made every effort to provide assistance, there is a shortage of food and funds. The future deaths of disaster victims in the county are unimaginable.

We sincerely hope that philanthropists at home and abroad will provide assistance.

Number of Visitors to Concession Prisons

Limited to Only Six People Per Day

The Department of General Affairs of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs previously sent a letter to the Shanghai office, stating that the Central Army Prison Guard Training Class would send 70 trainees to Shanghai to visit the concession prisons. Yesterday, the Provisional Court sent Official Letter No. 666 to the Ministry's office, stating that the court welcomes the trainees from the Central Army Prison Guard Training Class to visit the prisons in the concession. However, only the women's prison and the civil detention center are affiliated with this court. The other concession prisons are managed by the Municipal Council, and personnel have been sent to negotiate. According to the reply, in accordance with the concession prison regulations, the number of visitors per day is limited to six. In addition to sending personnel to inform your office of everything in person, this letter is sent in reply for your information. It is hoped that after the trainees arrive in Shanghai, you will confirm the date of the visit in advance and notify this court so that it can inform the Municipal Council for reference. After receiving the letter, the office immediately sent a letter to the General Affairs Department of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs for review and action.
